    23	
    24	func installSignalHandler(p *tea.Program) func() {
    25	        ch := make(chan struct{})
    26	
    27	        go func() {
    28	                sig := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
    29	                signal.Notify(sig, os.Interrupt, syscall.SIGTERM)
    30	
    31	                defer func() {
    32	                        signal.Stop(sig)
    33	                        close(ch)
    34	                }()
    35	
    36	                for {
    37	                        select {
    38	                        case <-ch:
    39	                                return
    40	
    41	                        case <-sig:
    42	                                p.Send(terminateMsg{})
    43	                        }
    44	                }
    45	        }()
    46	
    47	        return func() {
    48	                ch <- struct{}{}
    49	        }
    50	}

    52	type SelectOptions struct {
    53	        Options []string
    54	        // Default will be highlighted first if it's a valid option.
    55	        Default    string
    56	        Message    string
    57	        Size       int
    58	        HideSearch bool
    59	}

    61	type RichSelectOptions struct {
    62	        Options    []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
    63	        Default    string
    64	        Size       int
    65	        HideSearch bool
    66	}
    67	
    68	// RichSelect displays a list of user options including name and description.
    69	func RichSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichSelectOptions) (*codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption, error) {
    70	        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
    71	        var defaultOpt string
    72	        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
    73	                line := option.Name
    74	                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
    75	                        line += ": " + option.Description
    76	                }
    77	                opts[i] = line
    78	
    79	                if option.Value == richOptions.Default {
    80	                        defaultOpt = line
    81	                }
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        selected, err := Select(inv, SelectOptions{
    85	                Options:    opts,
    86	                Default:    defaultOpt,
    87	                Size:       richOptions.Size,
    88	                HideSearch: richOptions.HideSearch,
    89	        })
    90	        if err != nil {
    91	                return nil, err
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        for i, option := range opts {
    95	                if option == selected {
    96	                        return &richOptions.Options[i], nil
    97	                }
    98	        }
    99	        return nil, xerrors.Errorf("unknown option selected: %s", selected)
   100	}
   101	
   102	// Select displays a list of user options.
   103	func Select(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts SelectOptions) (string, error) {
   104	        // The survey library used *always* fails when testing on Windows,
   105	        // as it requires a live TTY (can't be a conpty). We should fork
   106	        // this library to add a dummy fallback, that simply reads/writes
   107	        // to the IO provided. See:
   108	        // https://github.com/AlecAivazis/survey/blob/master/terminal/runereader_windows.go#L94
   109	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   110	                return opts.Options[0], nil
   111	        }
   112	
   113	        initialModel := selectModel{
   114	                search:     textinput.New(),
   115	                hideSearch: opts.HideSearch,
   116	                options:    opts.Options,
   117	                height:     opts.Size,
   118	                message:    opts.Message,
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        if initialModel.height == 0 {
   122	                initialModel.height = defaultSelectModelHeight
   123	        }
   124	
   125	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   126	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   127	
   128	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   129	                initialModel,
   130	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   131	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   132	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   133	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   134	        )
   135	
   136	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   137	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   138	
   139	        m, err := p.Run()
   140	        if err != nil {
   141	                return "", err
   142	        }
   143	
   144	        model, ok := m.(selectModel)
   145	        if !ok {
   146	                return "", xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        if model.canceled {
   150	                return "", ErrCanceled
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        return model.selected, nil
   154	}

   156	type selectModel struct {
   157	        search     textinput.Model
   158	        options    []string
   159	        cursor     int
   160	        height     int
   161	        message    string
   162	        selected   string
   163	        canceled   bool
   164	        hideSearch bool
   165	}
   166	
   167	func (selectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   168	        return nil
   169	}
   170	
   171	//nolint:revive // The linter complains about modifying 'm' but this is typical practice for bubbletea
   172	func (m selectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   173	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   174	
   175	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   176	        case terminateMsg:
   177	                m.canceled = true
   178	                return m, tea.Quit
   179	
   180	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   181	                switch msg.Type {
   182	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   183	                        m.canceled = true
   184	                        return m, tea.Quit
   185	
   186	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   187	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   188	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   189	                                m.selected = options[m.cursor]
   190	                                return m, tea.Quit
   191	                        }
   192	
   193	                case tea.KeyUp:
   194	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   195	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   196	                                m.cursor--
   197	                        } else {
   198	                                m.cursor = len(options) - 1
   199	                        }
   200	
   201	                case tea.KeyDown:
   202	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   203	                        if m.cursor < len(options)-1 {
   204	                                m.cursor++
   205	                        } else {
   206	                                m.cursor = 0
   207	                        }
   208	                }
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        if !m.hideSearch {
   212	                oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   213	                m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   214	
   215	                // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   216	                // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   217	                if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   218	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   219	
   220	                        if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   221	                                m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   222	                        }
   223	                }
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        return m, cmd
   227	}
   228	
   229	func (m selectModel) View() string {
   230	        var s strings.Builder
   231	
   232	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   233	
   234	        if m.selected != "" {
   235	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, m.selected)
   236	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   237	
   238	                return s.String()
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        if m.hideSearch {
   242	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s [Use arrows to move]\n", msg))
   243	        } else {
   244	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   245	                        "%s %s[Use arrows to move, type to filter]\n",
   246	                        msg,
   247	                        m.search.View(),
   248	                ))
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        options, start := m.viewableOptions()
   252	
   253	        for i, option := range options {
   254	                // Is this the currently selected option?
   255	                style := pretty.Wrap("  ", "")
   256	                if m.cursor == start+i {
   257	                        style = pretty.Style{
   258	                                pretty.Wrap("> ", ""),
   259	                                DefaultStyles.Keyword,
   260	                        }
   261	                }
   262	
   263	                _, _ = s.WriteString(pretty.Sprint(style, option))
   264	                _, _ = s.WriteString("\n")
   265	        }
   266	
   267	        return s.String()
   268	}
   269	
   270	func (m selectModel) viewableOptions() ([]string, int) {
   271	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   272	        halfHeight := m.height / 2
   273	        bottom := 0
   274	        top := len(options)
   275	
   276	        switch {
   277	        case m.cursor <= halfHeight:
   278	                top = min(top, m.height)
   279	        case m.cursor < top-halfHeight:
   280	                bottom = max(0, m.cursor-halfHeight)
   281	                top = min(top, m.cursor+halfHeight+1)
   282	        default:
   283	                bottom = max(0, top-m.height)
   284	        }
   285	
   286	        return options[bottom:top], bottom
   287	}
   288	
   289	func (m selectModel) filteredOptions() []string {
   290	        options := []string{}
   291	        for _, o := range m.options {
   292	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   293	                option := strings.ToLower(o)
   294	
   295	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   296	                        options = append(options, o)
   297	                }
   298	        }
   299	        return options
   300	}
   301	
   302	type MultiSelectOptions struct {
   303	        Message           string
   304	        Options           []string
   305	        Defaults          []string
   306	        EnableCustomInput bool
   307	}
   308	
   309	func MultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts MultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
   310	        // Similar hack is applied to Select()
   311	        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
   312	                return opts.Defaults, nil
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        options := make([]*multiSelectOption, len(opts.Options))
   316	        for i, option := range opts.Options {
   317	                chosen := false
   318	                for _, d := range opts.Defaults {
   319	                        if option == d {
   320	                                chosen = true
   321	                                break
   322	                        }
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                options[i] = &multiSelectOption{
   326	                        option: option,
   327	                        chosen: chosen,
   328	                }
   329	        }
   330	
   331	        initialModel := multiSelectModel{
   332	                search:            textinput.New(),
   333	                options:           options,
   334	                message:           opts.Message,
   335	                enableCustomInput: opts.EnableCustomInput,
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
   339	        initialModel.search.Focus()
   340	
   341	        p := tea.NewProgram(
   342	                initialModel,
   343	                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
   344	                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
   345	                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
   346	                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
   347	        )
   348	
   349	        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
   350	        defer closeSignalHandler()
   351	
   352	        m, err := p.Run()
   353	        if err != nil {
   354	                return nil, err
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
   358	        if !ok {
   359	                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
   360	        }
   361	
   362	        if model.canceled {
   363	                return nil, ErrCanceled
   364	        }
   365	
   366	        return model.selectedOptions(), nil
   367	}
   368	
   369	type multiSelectOption struct {
   370	        option string
   371	        chosen bool
   372	}
   373	
   374	type multiSelectModel struct {
   375	        search            textinput.Model
   376	        options           []*multiSelectOption
   377	        cursor            int
   378	        message           string
   379	        canceled          bool
   380	        selected          bool
   381	        isCustomInputMode bool   // track if we're adding a custom option
   382	        customInput       string // store custom input
   383	        enableCustomInput bool   // control whether custom input is allowed
   384	}
   385	
   386	func (multiSelectModel) Init() tea.Cmd {
   387	        return nil
   388	}
   389	
   390	//nolint:revive // For same reason as previous Update definition
   391	func (m multiSelectModel) Update(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   392	        var cmd tea.Cmd
   393	
   394	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   395	                return m.handleCustomInputMode(msg)
   396	        }
   397	
   398	        switch msg := msg.(type) {
   399	        case terminateMsg:
   400	                m.canceled = true
   401	                return m, tea.Quit
   402	
   403	        case tea.KeyMsg:
   404	                switch msg.Type {
   405	                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   406	                        m.canceled = true
   407	                        return m, tea.Quit
   408	
   409	                case tea.KeyEnter:
   410	                        // Switch to custom input mode if we're on the "+ Add custom value:" option
   411	                        if m.enableCustomInput && m.cursor == len(m.filteredOptions()) {
   412	                                m.isCustomInputMode = true
   413	                                return m, nil
   414	                        }
   415	                        if len(m.options) != 0 {
   416	                                m.selected = true
   417	                                return m, tea.Quit
   418	                        }
   419	
   420	                case tea.KeySpace:
   421	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   422	                        if len(options) != 0 {
   423	                                options[m.cursor].chosen = !options[m.cursor].chosen
   424	                        }
   425	                        // We back out early here otherwise a space will be inserted
   426	                        // into the search field.
   427	                        return m, nil
   428	
   429	                case tea.KeyUp:
   430	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   431	                        if m.cursor > 0 {
   432	                                m.cursor--
   433	                        } else {
   434	                                m.cursor = maxIndex
   435	                        }
   436	
   437	                case tea.KeyDown:
   438	                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
   439	                        if m.cursor < maxIndex {
   440	                                m.cursor++
   441	                        } else {
   442	                                m.cursor = 0
   443	                        }
   444	
   445	                case tea.KeyRight:
   446	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   447	                        for _, option := range options {
   448	                                option.chosen = true
   449	                        }
   450	
   451	                case tea.KeyLeft:
   452	                        options := m.filteredOptions()
   453	                        for _, option := range options {
   454	                                option.chosen = false
   455	                        }
   456	                }
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        oldSearch := m.search.Value()
   460	        m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
   461	
   462	        // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
   463	        // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
   464	        if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
   465	                options := m.filteredOptions()
   466	                if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
   467	                        m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
   468	                }
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        return m, cmd
   472	}
   473	
   474	func (m multiSelectModel) getMaxIndex() int {
   475	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   476	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   477	                // Include the "+ Add custom value" entry
   478	                return len(options)
   479	        }
   480	        // Includes only the actual options
   481	        return len(options) - 1
   482	}
   483	
   484	// handleCustomInputMode manages keyboard interactions when in custom input mode
   485	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputMode(msg tea.Msg) (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   486	        keyMsg, ok := msg.(tea.KeyMsg)
   487	        if !ok {
   488	                return m, nil
   489	        }
   490	
   491	        switch keyMsg.Type {
   492	        case tea.KeyEnter:
   493	                return m.handleCustomInputSubmission()
   494	
   495	        case tea.KeyCtrlC:
   496	                m.canceled = true
   497	                return m, tea.Quit
   498	
   499	        case tea.KeyBackspace:
   500	                return m.handleCustomInputBackspace()
   501	
   502	        default:
   503	                m.customInput += keyMsg.String()
   504	                return m, nil
   505	        }
   506	}
   507	
   508	// handleCustomInputSubmission processes the submission of custom input
   509	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputSubmission() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   510	        if m.customInput == "" {
   511	                m.isCustomInputMode = false
   512	                return m, nil
   513	        }
   514	
   515	        // Clear search to ensure option is visible and cursor points to the new option
   516	        m.search.SetValue("")
   517	
   518	        // Check for duplicates
   519	        for i, opt := range m.options {
   520	                if opt.option == m.customInput {
   521	                        // If the option exists but isn't chosen, select it
   522	                        if !opt.chosen {
   523	                                opt.chosen = true
   524	                        }
   525	
   526	                        // Point cursor to the new option
   527	                        m.cursor = i
   528	
   529	                        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   530	                        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   531	                        m.customInput = ""
   532	                        return m, nil
   533	                }
   534	        }
   535	
   536	        // Add new unique option
   537	        m.options = append(m.options, &multiSelectOption{
   538	                option: m.customInput,
   539	                chosen: true,
   540	        })
   541	
   542	        // Point cursor to the newly added option
   543	        m.cursor = len(m.options) - 1
   544	
   545	        // Reset custom input mode to disabled
   546	        m.customInput = ""
   547	        m.isCustomInputMode = false
   548	        return m, nil
   549	}
   550	
   551	// handleCustomInputBackspace handles backspace in custom input mode
   552	func (m *multiSelectModel) handleCustomInputBackspace() (tea.Model, tea.Cmd) {
   553	        if len(m.customInput) > 0 {
   554	                m.customInput = m.customInput[:len(m.customInput)-1]
   555	        }
   556	        return m, nil
   557	}
   558	
   559	func (m multiSelectModel) View() string {
   560	        var s strings.Builder
   561	
   562	        msg := pretty.Sprintf(pretty.Bold(), "? %s", m.message)
   563	
   564	        if m.selected {
   565	                selected := pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, strings.Join(m.selectedOptions(), ", "))
   566	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s %s\n", msg, selected))
   567	
   568	                return s.String()
   569	        }
   570	
   571	        if m.isCustomInputMode {
   572	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s\nEnter custom value: %s\n", msg, m.customInput))
   573	                return s.String()
   574	        }
   575	
   576	        _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   577	                "%s %s[Use arrows to move, space to select, <right> to all, <left> to none, type to filter]\n",
   578	                msg,
   579	                m.search.View(),
   580	        ))
   581	
   582	        options := m.filteredOptions()
   583	        for i, option := range options {
   584	                cursor := "  "
   585	                chosen := "[ ]"
   586	                o := option.option
   587	
   588	                if m.cursor == i {
   589	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   590	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[ ]")
   591	                        o = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, o)
   592	                }
   593	
   594	                if option.chosen {
   595	                        chosen = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "[x]")
   596	                }
   597	
   598	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(
   599	                        "%s%s %s\n",
   600	                        cursor,
   601	                        chosen,
   602	                        o,
   603	                ))
   604	        }
   605	
   606	        if m.enableCustomInput {
   607	                // Add the "+ Add custom value" option at the bottom
   608	                cursor := "  "
   609	                text := " + Add custom value"
   610	                if m.cursor == len(options) {
   611	                        cursor = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, "> ")
   612	                        text = pretty.Sprint(DefaultStyles.Keyword, text)
   613	                }
   614	                _, _ = s.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s%s\n", cursor, text))
   615	        }
   616	        return s.String()
   617	}
   618	
   619	func (m multiSelectModel) filteredOptions() []*multiSelectOption {
   620	        options := []*multiSelectOption{}
   621	        for _, o := range m.options {
   622	                filter := strings.ToLower(m.search.Value())
   623	                option := strings.ToLower(o.option)
   624	
   625	                if strings.Contains(option, filter) {
   626	                        options = append(options, o)
   627	                }
   628	        }
   629	        return options
   630	}
   631	
   632	func (m multiSelectModel) selectedOptions() []string {
   633	        selected := []string{}
   634	        for _, o := range m.options {
   635	                if o.chosen {
   636	                        selected = append(selected, o.option)
   637	                }
   638	        }
   639	        return selected
   640	}
   641

Now let me examine the issue more closely. Based on the PR description, there are two bugs:

1. MultiSelect does not present available options if the default is not set or is an empty array
2. MultiSelect ignores descriptions

Looking at the `parameter.go` file, I can see how `MultiSelect` is called:

```go
values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
    Options:  options,
    Defaults: options,
})
```

And in `select.go`, the `MultiSelect` function has these parameters:

```go
type MultiSelectOptions struct {
    Message           string
    Options          []string
    Defaults          []string
    EnableCustomInput bool
}
```

Now let me create a test script to reproduce the issue:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_multiselect.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
	"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
	"github.com/coder/serpent"
)

func main() {
	fmt.Println("Testing MultiSelect with empty defaults...")
	
	// Test case 1: Empty defaults (the bug)
	inv := &serpent.Invocation{}
	options := []string{"Option A", "Option B", "Option C"}
	
	fmt.Printf("Options: %v\n", options)
	fmt.Printf("Defaults: [] (empty)\n")
	
	// This should present all options but currently doesn'"'"'t work
	values, err := cliui.MultiSelect(inv, cliui.MultiSelectOptions{
		Options:  options,
		Defaults: []string{}, // Empty defaults
	})
	
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("Selected values: %v\n", values)
	}
	
	// Test case 2: MultiSelect with rich options (descriptions)
	fmt.Println("\nTesting MultiSelect with rich options (descriptions)...")
	
	// This simulates what happens in RichParameter function
	templateParam := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
		Type: "list(string)",
		Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
			{Name: "Option A", Value: "a", Description: "Description for A"},
			{Name: "Option B", Value: "b", Description: "Description for B"},
			{Name: "Option C", Value: "c", Description: "Description for C"},
		},
	}
	
	// This is how it'"'"'s currently called in parameter.go
	var richOptions []string
	for _, option := range templateParam.Options {
		richOptions = append(richOptions, option.Name)
		// Note: descriptions are ignored!
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Rich options: %v\n", richOptions)
	fmt.Println("Notice: Descriptions are not shown!")
	
	values2, err := cliui.MultiSelect(inv, cliui.MultiSelectOptions{
		Options:  richOptions,
		Defaults: richOptions,
	})
	
	if err != nil {
		fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("Selected rich values: %v\n", values2)
	}
}'

2026-01-08 08:07:22,950 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issues better. Let me analyze them:

**Issue 1: MultiSelect does not present available options if the default is not set or is an empty array**

Looking at the code, the problem is in `parameter.go` lines 41-49:
1. The `DefaultValue` field is unmarshaled into `options`
2. Both `Options` and `Defaults` parameters for `MultiSelect` are set to this same `options` array

If `DefaultValue` is empty (like `[]`), then `options` will be an empty array, and `MultiSelect` will be called with empty options, which won't present anything to the user.

**Issue 2: MultiSelect ignores descriptions**

Looking at how `RichSelect` works (lines 73-76 in `select.go`), it properly handles descriptions by including them in the display format. However, the `MultiSelect` in `parameter.go` only extracts the option names from `templateVersionParameter.Options` without including descriptions.

Let me create a more comprehensive test to understand the expected behavior:

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/analyze_issue.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
)

func main() {
	// Simulate different DefaultValue scenarios
	testCases := []struct {
		name         string
		defaultValue string
	}{
		{"Empty array", "[]"},
		{"Array with values", "[\"a\",\"b\",\"c\"]"},
		{"Empty string", ""},
		{"Null", "null"},
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		fmt.Printf("\nTest case: %s\n", tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", tc.defaultValue)

		var options []string
		err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.defaultValue), &options)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("Unmarshaled options: %v (len: %d)\n", options, len(options))
		}
	}

	// Analyze the second issue: descriptions
	fmt.Println("\n\nIssue 2: MultiSelect ignores descriptions")
	fmt.Println("Current approach in parameter.go:")
	fmt.Println("- Extracts only option names from templateVersionParameter.Options")
	fmt.Println("- Ignores descriptions completely")
	fmt.Println("\nRichSelect approach (works correctly):")
	fmt.Println("- Includes descriptions in display format: '"'"'Name: Description'"'"'")
	fmt.Println("- Returns the full TemplateVersionParameterOption object")
}'

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/cli/cliui/select.go   --old_str 'func MultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, opts MultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
        // Similar hack is applied to Select()
        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
                return opts.Defaults, nil
        }

        options := make([]*multiSelectOption, len(opts.Options))
        for i, option := range opts.Options {
                chosen := false
                for _, d := range opts.Defaults {
                        if option == d {
                                chosen = true
                                break
                        }
                }

                options[i] = &multiSelectOption{
                        option: option,
                        chosen: chosen,
                }
        }

        initialModel := multiSelectModel{
                search:            textinput.New(),
                options:           options,
                message:           opts.Message,
                enableCustomInput: opts.EnableCustomInput,
        }

        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
        initialModel.search.Focus()

        p := tea.NewProgram(
                initialModel,
                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
        )

        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
        defer closeSignalHandler()

        m, err := p.Run()
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
        if !ok {
                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
        }

        if model.canceled {
                return nil, ErrCanceled
        }

        return model.selectedOptions(), nil

                chosen := false
                for _, d := range opts.Defaults {
                        if option == d {
                                chosen = true
                                break
                        }
                }

                options[i] = &multiSelectOption{
                        option: option,
                        chosen: chosen,
                }
        }

        initialModel := multiSelectModel{
                search:            textinput.New(),
                options:           options,
                message:           opts.Message,
                enableCustomInput: opts.EnableCustomInput,
        }

        initialModel.search.Prompt = ""
        initialModel.search.Focus()

        p := tea.NewProgram(
                initialModel,
                tea.WithoutSignalHandler(),
                tea.WithContext(inv.Context()),
                tea.WithInput(inv.Stdin),
                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
        )

        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
        defer closeSignalHandler()

        m, err := p.Run()
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
        if !ok {
                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
        }

        if model.canceled {
                return nil, ErrCanceled
        }

        return model.selectedOptions(), nil
}

// RichMultiSelect displays a list of user options including name and description for multi-select.
func RichMultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichMultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
                line := option.Name
                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
                        line += ": " + option.Description
                }
                opts[i] = line
        }

        selected, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
                Message:           richOptions.Message,
                Options:           opts,
                Defaults:          richOptions.Defaults,
                EnableCustomInput: richOptions.EnableCustomInput,
        })
        if err != nil {
                return nil, err
        }

        // Convert back to the actual option values
        var values []string
        for _, sel := range selected {
                // Extract the name part before any colon (for description separation)
                name := sel
                if idx := strings.Index(sel, ": "); idx != -1 {
                        name = sel[:idx]
                }
                
                // Find the corresponding option
                for _, option := range richOptions.Options {
                        if option.Name == name {
                                values = append(values, option.Value)
                                break
                        }
                }
        }
        return values, nil
}'

    58	        DisplayName          string `json:"display_name,omitempty"`
    59	        Description          string `json:"description"`
    60	        DescriptionPlaintext string `json:"description_plaintext"`
    61	        Type                 string `json:"type" enums:"string,number,bool,list(string)"`
    62	        // FormType has an enum value of empty string, `""`.
    63	        // Keep the leading comma in the enums struct tag.
    64	        FormType            string                           `json:"form_type" enums:",radio,dropdown,input,textarea,slider,checkbox,switch,tag-select,multi-select,error"`
    65	        Mutable             bool                             `json:"mutable"`
    66	        DefaultValue        string                           `json:"default_value"`
    67	        Icon                string                           `json:"icon"`
    68	        Options             []TemplateVersionParameterOption `json:"options"`
    69	        ValidationError     string                           `json:"validation_error,omitempty"`
    70	        ValidationRegex     string                           `json:"validation_regex,omitempty"`
    71	        ValidationMin       *int32                           `json:"validation_min,omitempty"`
    72	        ValidationMax       *int32                           `json:"validation_max,omitempty"`
    73	        ValidationMonotonic ValidationMonotonicOrder         `json:"validation_monotonic,omitempty" enums:"increasing,decreasing"`
    74	        Required            bool                             `json:"required"`
    75	        Ephemeral           bool                             `json:"ephemeral"`
    76	}
    77	
    78	// TemplateVersionParameterOption represents a selectable option for a template parameter.
    79	type TemplateVersionParameterOption struct {
    80	        Name        string `json:"name"`
    81	        Description string `json:"description"`
    82	        Value       string `json:"value"`
    83	        Icon        string `json:"icon"`
    84	}
    85	
    86	// TemplateVersionVariable represents a managed template variable.
    87	type TemplateVersionVariable struct {
    88	        Name         string `json:"name"`
    89	        Description  string `json:"description"`
    90	        Type         string `json:"type" enums:"string,number,bool"`
    91	        Value        string `json:"value"`
    92	        DefaultValue string `json:"default_value"`
    93	        Required     bool   `json:"required"`
    94	        Sensitive    bool   `json:"sensitive"`
    95	}

import (
	"encoding/json"

func main() {
	// Test Case 1: Empty defaults (the main bug)
	fmt.Println("=== Test Case 1: Empty defaults ===")

}

func testEmptyDefaults() {
	// Simulate the scenario where DefaultValue is empty or "[]"
	testParams := []struct {
		name         string
		defaultValue string
		expectedErr  bool
	}{
		{"Empty array JSON", "[]", false},
		{"Null JSON", "null", false},
		{"Empty string", "", false},
		{"Array with values", `["a","b","c"]`, false},
	}

	for _, tc := range testParams {
		fmt.Printf("\nTesting %s:\n", tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", tc.defaultValue)

		var defaultValues []string
		if tc.defaultValue != "" {
			err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.defaultValue), &defaultValues)
			if err != nil {
				fmt.Printf("❌ Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
				continue
			}
		}

		fmt.Printf("✅ Parsed defaultValues: %v (len: %d)\n", defaultValues, len(defaultValues))

		// Simulate what our fixed code would do
		if len(defaultValues) > 0 {
			fmt.Printf("✅ Would use MultiSelect with Options = Defaults = %v\n", defaultValues)
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("⚠️  No default values, need TemplateVersionParameter.Options\n")
		}
	}
}

func testWithDescriptions() {
	// Test rich options with descriptions
	richOptions := []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
		{Name: "Frontend", Value: "frontend", Description: "React/Vue/Angular applications"},
		{Name: "Backend", Value: "backend", Description: "API servers and microservices"},
		{Name: "Database", Value: "database", Description: "PostgreSQL/MySQL databases"},
	}

	fmt.Printf("Rich options available:\n")
	for _, opt := range richOptions {
		fmt.Printf("  - %s: %s (value: %s)\n", opt.Name, opt.Description, opt.Value)
	}

	// Current approach (broken): only shows names
	currentOptions := []string{"Frontend", "Backend", "Database"}
	fmt.Printf("\nCurrent approach (ignores descriptions): %v\n", currentOptions)

	// New approach: shows name + description
	newOptions := make([]string, len(richOptions))
	for i, option := range richOptions {
		line := option.Name
		if len(option.Description) > 0 {
			line += ": " + option.Description
		}
		newOptions[i] = line
	}
	fmt.Printf("Fixed approach (includes descriptions): %v\n", newOptions)
}

func testNormalCase() {
	// Test that our fix doesn'"'"'t break normal functionality
	templateParam := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
		Name:          "test-param",
		Type:          "list(string)",
		DefaultValue:  `["opt1","opt2","opt3"]`,
		Options:       []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{},
	}

	fmt.Printf("Template parameter: %s\n", templateParam.Name)
	fmt.Printf("Type: %s\n", templateParam.Type)
	fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", templateParam.DefaultValue)
	fmt.Printf("Options available: %d\n", len(templateParam.Options))

	// Our fix logic
	var defaultValues []string
	if templateParam.DefaultValue != "" {
		err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateParam.DefaultValue), &defaultValues)
		if err != nil {
			fmt.Printf("❌ Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
			return
		}
	}

	if len(templateParam.Options) > 0 {
		fmt.Printf("✅ Would use RichMultiSelect with %d rich options\n", len(templateParam.Options))
	} else if len(defaultValues) > 0 {
		fmt.Printf("✅ Would use regular MultiSelect with options: %v\n", defaultValues)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("❌ Error: no options available\n")
	}
}'

+package main

+func main() {
+// Simulate different DefaultValue scenarios
+testCases := []struct {
+name         string
+defaultValue string
+}{
+{"Empty array", "[]"},
+{"Array with values", "[\"a\",\"b\",\"c\"]"},
+{"Empty string", ""},
+{"Null", "null"},
+}
+
+for _, tc := range testCases {
+fmt.Printf("\nTest case: %s\n", tc.name)
+fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", tc.defaultValue)
+
+var options []string
+err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.defaultValue), &options)
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("Unmarshaled options: %v (len: %d)\n", options, len(options))
+}
+}
+
+// Analyze the second issue: descriptions
+fmt.Println("\n\nIssue 2: MultiSelect ignores descriptions")
+fmt.Println("Current approach in parameter.go:")
+fmt.Println("- Extracts only option names from templateVersionParameter.Options")
+fmt.Println("- Ignores descriptions completely")
+fmt.Println("\nRichSelect approach (works correctly):")
+fmt.Println("- Includes descriptions in display format: 'Name: Description'")
+fmt.Println("- Returns the full TemplateVersionParameterOption object")
+}

+        }
+

+                return "", ErrCanceled
+        }

+                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
+        )
+
+        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
+        defer closeSignalHandler()
+
+        m, err := p.Run()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
+        if !ok {
+                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
+        }
+
+        if model.canceled {
+                return nil, ErrCanceled
+        }
+
+        return model.selectedOptions(), nil
+}

+// RichMultiSelect displays a list of user options including name and description for multi-select.
+func RichMultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichMultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
+        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
+        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
+                line := option.Name
+                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
+                        line += ": " + option.Description
+                }
+                opts[i] = line
+        }
+
+        selected, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
+                Message:           richOptions.Message,
+                Options:           opts,
+                Defaults:          richOptions.Defaults,
+                EnableCustomInput: richOptions.EnableCustomInput,
+        })
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        // Convert back to the actual option values
+        var values []string
+        for _, sel := range selected {
+                // Extract the name part before any colon (for description separation)
+                name := sel
+                if idx := strings.Index(sel, ": "); idx != -1 {
+                        name = sel[:idx]
+                }
+                
+                // Find the corresponding option
+                for _, option := range richOptions.Options {
+                        if option.Name == name {
+                                values = append(values, option.Value)
+                                break
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        return values, nil
 }

+func main() {
+// Test Case 1: Empty defaults (the main bug)
+fmt.Println("=== Test Case 1: Empty defaults ===")
+testEmptyDefaults()
+
+// Test Case 2: MultiSelect with descriptions (second bug) 
+fmt.Println("\n=== Test Case 2: MultiSelect with descriptions ===")
+testWithDescriptions()
+
+// Test Case 3: Normal case with defaults
+fmt.Println("\n=== Test Case 3: Normal case with defaults ===")
+testNormalCase()

+func testEmptyDefaults() {
+// Simulate the scenario where DefaultValue is empty or "[]"
+testParams := []struct {
+name         string
+defaultValue string
+expectedErr  bool
+}{
+{"Empty array JSON", "[]", false},
+{"Null JSON", "null", false},
+{"Empty string", "", false},
+{"Array with values", `["a","b","c"]`, false},
+}
+
+for _, tc := range testParams {
+fmt.Printf("\nTesting %s:\n", tc.name)
+fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", tc.defaultValue)
+
+var defaultValues []string
+if tc.defaultValue != "" {
+err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(tc.defaultValue), &defaultValues)
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("❌ Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
+continue
+}
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("✅ Parsed defaultValues: %v (len: %d)\n", defaultValues, len(defaultValues))
+
+// Simulate what our fixed code would do
+if len(defaultValues) > 0 {
+fmt.Printf("✅ Would use MultiSelect with Options = Defaults = %v\n", defaultValues)
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("⚠️  No default values, need TemplateVersionParameter.Options\n")
+}
+}
+}
+
+func testWithDescriptions() {
+// Test rich options with descriptions
+richOptions := []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Frontend", Value: "frontend", Description: "React/Vue/Angular applications"},
+{Name: "Backend", Value: "backend", Description: "API servers and microservices"},
+{Name: "Database", Value: "database", Description: "PostgreSQL/MySQL databases"},
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Rich options available:\n")
+for _, opt := range richOptions {
+fmt.Printf("  - %s: %s (value: %s)\n", opt.Name, opt.Description, opt.Value)
+}
+
+// Current approach (broken): only shows names
+currentOptions := []string{"Frontend", "Backend", "Database"}
+fmt.Printf("\nCurrent approach (ignores descriptions): %v\n", currentOptions)
+
+// New approach: shows name + description
+newOptions := make([]string, len(richOptions))
+for i, option := range richOptions {
+line := option.Name
+if len(option.Description) > 0 {
+line += ": " + option.Description
+}
+newOptions[i] = line
+}
+fmt.Printf("Fixed approach (includes descriptions): %v\n", newOptions)
+}
+
+func testNormalCase() {
+// Test that our fix doesn't break normal functionality
+templateParam := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:          "test-param",
+Type:          "list(string)",
+DefaultValue:  `["opt1","opt2","opt3"]`,
+Options:       []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{},
+}
+
+fmt.Printf("Template parameter: %s\n", templateParam.Name)
+fmt.Printf("Type: %s\n", templateParam.Type)
+fmt.Printf("DefaultValue: %s\n", templateParam.DefaultValue)
+fmt.Printf("Options available: %d\n", len(templateParam.Options))
+
+// Our fix logic
+var defaultValues []string
+if templateParam.DefaultValue != "" {
+err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateParam.DefaultValue), &defaultValues)
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("❌ Error unmarshaling: %v\n", err)
+return
+}
+}
+
+if len(templateParam.Options) > 0 {
+fmt.Printf("✅ Would use RichMultiSelect with %d rich options\n", len(templateParam.Options))
+} else if len(defaultValues) > 0 {
+fmt.Printf("✅ Would use regular MultiSelect with options: %v\n", defaultValues)
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("❌ Error: no options available\n")
+}
+}
